Post Content: 
Before I start, as you can see I have posted this under "Pure massage only"...let's just say I am suspicious that I just missed out...

Anyway, decided to take a punt today at this place. Haven't been there before, but had seen it advertised in The Tele under good old "Health Beauty & Fitness".

It is located just a couple of mins walk from the station, at the base of a relatively new unit block.

Upon approach it appeared to have all the signs of an "extras" establishment - no sign stating "Health Rebates Available", not appearing to be an overly professional setup, and not appearing to be targeted at women. As I got closer, the young "casually dressed" ladies I could see through the window only reaffirmed my belief I was in for some extras.

I enter...mamasan shows me to a room...asks me how long? I ask how much? Mamasan advises 30 for 30mins, 50 for 60 mins. Me say 60 mins please.

A young fairly good looking chinese girl enters the room. She is wearing 'short' shorts, a jacket over a singlet top with a hint of cleavage. This is all looking good.

I strip off, lie down and the massage begins...

She starts with my back, on to the back of the legs, works my neck...but no oil?!?! But wait, after about 30 mins with me still lying on my back...here comes the oil!! Appears we may be back on track!

The young lady gets to work massaging my back using the oil. Another 10 mins passes. Hang on, she moves to the back of my legs...will there be any tackle tickle I ask myself???

At the back end of another 10 mins of back of the leg massaging, there is the slightest tackle tickle. I am thinking that although time appears to be running out, I am still in with a shot for some extras.

She leaves the room...hot towel perhaps followed by the "roll over please" I think to myself. She returns, and yes, she has a hot towel. She wipes the oil from my body. Now just waiting for the green light.....but no...she starts massaging my bloody head!!

All this time I was unable to see the clock, so I am hoping that my 'gut feel' on how long had passed was off the mark. As it would turn out, it was just about spot on, as after about 10 mins of bloody head massaging the young girl proclaims "time's up!".

Not willing to give up that easily, thinking that this may be a ploy on her behalf to get me to pay for another half hour plus 'extras', I ask "Do you offer any extras?". No, she insists looking all shy. How about the other girls, do any of them offer extras? No, she insists even more convincingly.

God damn!!!

Insult to injury as I exiting this joint I pass 4 young ML's in the entry foyer who all look like they are dressed for a brothel.

Have I missed something? Have I developed dog breath overnight?? All these years that I've been looking into the mirror telling myself that I'm not ugly, but in fact I actually make The Elephant Man look like Miss Universe???

This place has absolutely got me stuffed!! The only theory I have left is that this girl was on her 1st day and the other girls hadn't let her into 'the secret'.

Would appreciate if anyone else has been here and can share their experiences.....

Oh well, off to King St Newtown then...
